with fixed \(a=0.11423898258902421,\; B=40.69810220267985,\; k=0.08368363514073095\).

So GT has these structural properties:

- As a function of \(t\): it contains **exactly one non-polynomial \(t\)-dependence**, namely \(aP e^{-kt}\). No \(\log t\), no \(t\), no \(t^p\), no \(e^{+kt}\), no \(1/t^5\), etc.
- As a function of \(P\): it contains a **polynomial part** \(a(2P - P^2/B)\) plus a **non-polynomial part** \(-aP e^{-kP}\). So it involves \(P e^{-kP}\) (an exponential in \(P\)), and also a \(P e^{-kt}\) term (exponential in \(t\) multiplied by \(P\)).

A candidate can only match if it can simultaneously produce:
1) a term proportional to \(P e^{-kt}\) (exponential decay in \(t\) with coefficient linear in \(P\)), and  
2) a term proportional to \(-P e^{-kP}\) (exponential decay in \(P\) multiplied by \(P\)), and  
3) the polynomial terms \(+(\text{const})P\) and \(-(\text{const})P^2\).

## GT Analysis

The GT expression is:
```
0.11424*(1 - P/40.698)*P + 0.11424*(1 - exp(-0.08368*P))*P + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

Expanding:
```
0.11424*P - 0.11424*P²/40.698 + 0.11424*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

Simplifying:
```
-0.002807*P² + 0.22848*P - 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*P) + 0.11424*P*exp(-0.08368*t)
```

The GT has these basis functions:
1. **P²** term
2. **P** term (linear)
3. **P·exp(-αP)** term — a product of P and an exponential in P
4. **P·exp(-αt)** term — a product of P and an exponential in t

This is critical: the GT contains `P*exp(-c*P)` and `P*exp(-c*t)` as essential basis functions.

Let me now check each candidate:

### Candidate 1:
`P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*Max(0, P+c3) + c4*log(P*c5+1)*log(c6*t+1) + c7*cos(c8*log(c9*t+1))`

Basis functions: P², P, Max(0,...), log()*log(), cos(log()). Missing P*exp(-cP) and P*exp(-ct). The log and cos terms cannot replicate exponentials exactly.

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2:
`P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*Max(0, P+c3) + c4*log(P*c5+1)*log(c6*t+1) + c7*(P*c8+1)^c9`

Missing P*exp(-cP) and P*exp(-ct). Power functions and logs can't replicate these.

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 3:
`P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + P^c3*c4*t^c5 + c6*t + c7`

Has P^c3*t^c5 which is a power law, not matching exp(-cP) or exp(-ct).

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4:
`P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2*c3 + c4*Max(0, P+c5) + c6 + c7*log(P*c8+1)*log(c9*t+1)`

Missing exp terms. Log products can't match exp(-cP) or exp(-ct).

### Candidate 39:
`P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*log(c3*exp(c4*|P|)+1) + c5*t + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)*log(P*c9+1)`

Let me analyze: P*c2*log(c3*exp(c4*P)+1). For P≥0, if c4<0, say c4=-α: log(c3*exp(-αP)+1). For large P, this → 0, for P=0, log(c3+1). This is NOT the same as P*exp(-αP).

## Summary

The GT contains essential basis functions P*exp(-αP) and P*exp(-αt) that are exponential in nature. None of the candidates contain both of these basis functions simultaneously. Most candidates use polynomials, logarithms, power laws, rational functions, or piecewise functions that cannot exactly replicate exponential decay terms.
